msg:As a hotel lover, I checked in at the Westin Financial Street Hotel this time. The suite I booked on Ctrip was not a square room type, so I paid extra to upgrade to an executive suite with a square room type.

When checking in, the front desk said: Sorry it's too late today, I will send a fruit plate to your room tomorrow.

I thought to myself that the fruit plate and welcome gifts should all be arranged in the room before the suite is checked in, and even if the guest changes rooms temporarily, they will be quickly added to the new room. Why did she say "it's late today", it's not already nine or ten o'clock in the evening.

Because it was my first time staying at this hotel in Financial Street, I didn't say anything. I thought tomorrow would be tomorrow.

So, I checked into a big old suite with no welcome gift. Maybe the hotel has not been renovated for many years and is very old.

When I returned to the room the next night, the fruit plate mentioned by the front desk was still nowhere to be found. Don't expect other welcome gifts. Even the executive lounge trea**ent was something I asked the front desk for myself. I was thinking that if I didn't take the initiative to ask for it, I might not be given it.

The breakfast in the executive lounge is not very varied and the quality is worrying. I ordered an egg roll and it came out in an unknown shape.

Overall, the hotel is in a good location, next to the Financial Street Shopping Center, but the traffic is a bit awkward, between two subway stations. This is a hotel with few services, and the room service response is relatively slow.

When we got to the room, the cleaning staff came to help us with the extra bed.
